Hey! We are renting out a single room in our lovely flat in Moabit for July & August (2 months only).

The room comes with a bed, desk, a cupboard, and a clothes rack – plenty of space to store your stuff.
No bedding provided, so bring your own pillows and blankets.

You’ll be sharing the flat with two friendly women in their late 20s – both speak German and English, and the flat is LGBT+ friendly.

It’s a quiet, tidy and chilled household – ideal for someone looking for a peaceful place to stay short-term.
There’s a shared kitchen and bathroom, and the apartment is non-smoking.

Great location – close to a Ring-Bahn and U-Bahn (U9) stations plus a supermarket around the corner.

Message me if you're interested or have any questions!

[2026-06-12] A very Special Call Today:

"No one here gets out alive"

Tod, Trauer und Tiefe Verbindung

Wenn Tod in unser Leben tritt verändert sich alles auf einmal. Ob er an unsere eigene Türe klopft oder geliebte Menschen abholt, die Trauer legt sich wie ein Schleier auf unsere Weltempfidung.

Unsere Kultur bietet wenig Raum für Trauer oder Intimität mit Tod, und wir werden alleine gelassen mit einem überfordernden Prozess und überwältigenden Gefühlen. 

Viele andere Kuluren wissen, dass Trauer Gemeinschaft braucht, gehalten und gesehen werden will, damit wir sie verarbeiten können. 

Wir wollen dir deshalb Raum bieten mit deiner Trauer in den Kreis zu kommen, damit wir gemeinsam tragen können, was alleine viel zu schwer ist.

Am Freitag den 12. Juni laden wir zunächst zu einem online Kreis ein, zum teilen, gesehen und gehört werden. Hier können wir auch besprechen, was gebraucht wird als Begleitung um uns vorzubereiten auf diesen letzten Trip unser geliebten Menschen.

Please PM for the Call Details:

Time: Today Friday : 7-8 p.m.

[2026-06-11] **- S O L S T I C E  J A M -**
21st June Sunday 19.30-22.45
tg: https://t.me/butohjam

**🌞 19.30-20.40 Opening workshop with Tiziana Longo 
**(Arrive 15min before, we start on time)

ABOUT THE FACILITATOR:

**Tiziana Longo **is a performing artist, Butoh dancer, and teacher with over two decades of dedicated practice, including five years in Japan studying and assisting Yoshito Ohno at the Kazuo Ohno Studio.
Her work is grounded in embodiment and the continuous transformation of the body through memory, matter, texture, and imagination. Rather than expressing a fixed identity, her practice invites the body to become a vessel for multiple presences, unfolding as a living poetry in motion.
She is also a trauma-informed movement trainer specializing in TRE®, pelvic floor awareness, and embodied release practices, and the author of two forthcoming books.
www.longotiziana.com

ABOUT THE CLASS:

This workshop offers an introduction to Butoh through the awakening of sensorial perception, embodiment, and presence.
We begin by cultivating awareness of the body's relationship to space, gravity, and time through touch, listening, and direct experience. Particular attention is given to the feet as a point of contact with the earth, to the skin as a living boundary, and to the ears as organs of listening to both the inner and outer environment. Through these subtle practices, participants develop a deeper sensitivity to themselves, to others, and to the space around them.
From this foundation, we gradually enter a process of transformation. Through imagination, memory, textures, images, and states of being, the body is invited to move beyond habitual patterns and fixed identities. Rather than seeking to produce movement, participants are invited to cultivate presence and discover how movement naturally emerges when the body becomes receptive to what wishes to inhabit it.
Open to all levels of experience, this workshop offers a space for deep listening, creativity, and embodied discovery, where movement unfolds as a living poetry in motion.

**🌞 20:45-22:45 Butoh jam**
Looking forward to see you there!

[2026-06-10] Hi ich leite das hier nur weiter. Kontaktdaten unten :)

Wir suchen eine dritte Person für eine Unternehmensgründung! 👋

Wir (Till & Katzer) arbeiten seit ein paar Monaten an Kibuto, einer Buchhaltungssoftware – aufbauend auf unserem Wissen und unseren Erfahrungen als Kassenwarte des Funkloch-Festivals. Der zentrale Baustein ist eine KI für den Zahlungsabgleich, die Till in seiner Masterarbeit entwickelt hat.

Aktuell bewerben wir uns für verschiedene Fördertöpfe (u. a. EXIST, AI-Nation Grant, BSS). Viele dieser Programme sind auf Dreierteams ausgelegt, deshalb suchen wir Unterstützung. Und ehrlich gesagt macht es zu dritt auch vieles andere leichter.

Zwei Voraussetzungen, die wirklich beide erfüllt sein müssen:

1. Akademischer Abschluss innerhalb der letzten fünf Jahre (Bachelor, Master oder PhD).
2. Bereitschaft, Vollzeit am Projekt zu arbeiten. Der Lebensunterhalt ist über die Förderung für mindestens ein Jahr abgedeckt.

Beide Voraussetzungen sind Auflagen der Förderprogramme und somit verpflichtend. Geplanter Start ist im kommenden Herbst/Winter in Vollzeit – allerdings solltest du auch schon vorher einiges an Zeit haben, um mit uns die Anträge zu vervollständigen und dich auf den aktuellen Stand des Projekts zu bringen.

Worauf es uns fachlich ankommt

Idealerweise kommst du aus der Buchhaltung bzw. dem Rechnungswesen. Alternativ hilfst du bei der technischen Umsetzung: Unser aktueller Stack für den Prototypen ist Python/Django mit Vanilla JavaScript im Frontend, aktuell SQLite (Wechsel auf Postgres steht an) und Docker auf einem VPS. Falls du weder aus der Buchhaltung kommst noch etwas mit dem Stack anfangen kannst, aber Bock auf das Projekt hast und die beiden Voraussetzungen erfüllst, melde dich trotzdem gerne.

Interesse? Dann schreib uns kurz, wer du bist und wie du dich einbringen könntest. Einen Lebenslauf kannst du gerne mitschicken, musst du aber nicht.

Leitet den Text auch gerne an alle weiter, die das interessieren könnte!

📅 Deadline: 01.07.2026
📧 E-Mail: till-hecht@[user].de

Till & Katzer

[2026-06-09] DORNBURN II - KICK-OFF CALL!!! 

Lovelies,

it's been a while. After we had to postpone of May event, we are very close to a solution. We have locked in September 11th to 13th for the 2nd edition of Dornburn. There are some tiny details to clear in the contract and we need to fill some final lead positions for Mauersegler e.V. to be ready to sign the contract. This time: no issues with permits, promised. The castle is ready for us. 

Now it is up to us to fill it with life. Here are some important steps how you can help:

* Re-acivate your Discord. This will be our main source of communication. Download the app, turn on notifications for the important channels and discuss with us
* First, head over to Discord and have a look at the announcement channel where we plan our kick off on Monday, 15th of June
* Spread the word: tell your friends to join Discord (https://discord.gg/7MmHyMCj), forward this mail, tell friends how cool Dornburn is. Srsly this is of utmost importance, as we have realized that quite some mails bounce or end up in spam folders
* Think of new friends or crews who could join us
* Consider taking a lead role, think about projects you want to bring to life etc.

We will announce this on our messenger channels, but keep in mind: these are for info only, not core organization channels.

We love you and cannot wait to see you on the other side

[2026-06-08] Hellow Lovely!

You are invited to an online Ranger Q&A session as a space to get an introduction to the role and ask any questions you might have. 

**Thursday, June 11th, 19:00**

https://zoom.us/j/95956940532?pwd=CicFQGSvLGZJl1HRSbgAtyB6KGxOXb.1

Code: 288016

This is especially useful for anyone who has never been a Ranger before or has not attended a Burn, but everyone is welcome, including those who have not yet signed up for a shift. There are still spots available 🙂

This is not a formal training, but an open session to get an overview of the role, clarify expectations, and address anything that feels unclear.
Please make sure to read the Ranger Manual beforehand so the session can focus on questions and exchange rather than covering all the basics. 
Experienced Kiezburn Rangers are welcome to contribute with knowledge and experience.

Manual: https://docs.google.com/document/d/1MooMrRTMQ9MnGoIs5ACEiAlEmhol_p4PtSVpqzhyg7c/edit?tab=t.0

If you absolutely cannot make it, join the Ranger Q&A on site:
Wednesday, June 24th, 12:00, in front of the Ranger HQ.

I look forward to seeing you there!

[2026-06-07] Today 14h:

"Mitigating the risk of extinction from AI should be a global priority alongside other societal-scale risks such as pandemics and nuclear war".
   -Center for AI Safety.

I'm very concerned about the future.  Based on current progress, artificial general intelligence could be reached within 4 -6 years. It could bring amazing abundance, but also a big risk of AGI leading to species level disaster.  Leading researchers agree that we need to slow down to ensure safety, but with corporate and geopolitical competitive pressure, shortcuts are encouraged and compromises safety.

In the best case, we will be transitioning our society more dramatically and quickly than the industrial revolution: most jobs will be replaced by AI, and mass retraining will be needed. It's already starting, a huge social challenge.  And today already, deep fakes of women, celebrities and politicians are already threatening our democracy.

We need international agreements to take away the competitive pressure so there is time to assure safety, and more.

So I have the following ideas:
- Join the demo on 5.6. 14h at the Kanzleramt:
 Come along?  https://fairnessjetzt.de/
- get informed to understand the problem:
  - Want to gather and watch "The AI Doc" together?  Our living room and projector could work.
  https://www.humanetech.com/landing/the-ai-doc

[2026-06-05] Hello everyone! I’m launching the final iteration of our social project at the Meaning Alignment Institute: **Something Real.**

It’s an event series where the night is decided entirely by the people in the room. You say what you want—your wildest idea, your deepest need—the community votes, and whatever wins, we do.

**How it works:**

**Propose an idea:** Follow the link below and tell us: What would make a Sunday night worth remembering? (An honest sharing circle? An ugly greeting card contest? An intellectual dinner?)

**Vote:** Back someone else's idea or push your own. Votes are counted and the winning theme is announced 2 days before the event!

**Show up: **Experience the winning concept brought to life

🔗 Propose & Vote Here: https://moe.events/berlin/fincan

(Note: While anyone can propose an idea, we have a budget to hire professional facilitators. If you have professional or certified experience running workshops, submit your concept — or even an experimental variation of it — and let's collaborate!)

[2026-06-05] Stammtisch News 
—————————————
Next Week: Thursday 11.06 - 19:00
—————————————-
(German below)
Dear Burners,
Our next Stammtisch will be at 19:00 in front of the Zwingli Church at Danneckerstraße, corner of Rudolfstraße (10245). (The Google Maps link is below, thanks Nikki).
We will meet at two tables you see on the picture. The benches should have space for 8 people without love, 12 people with love, or even more people with even more love. I can bring 2–4 folding chairs if someone wants to help me carry them from Simon-Dach-Straße and back. I will bring tablecloths and some romantic stuff.
Feel free to bring drinks and food. The nearest Späti is about a 3-minute walk away, so we won’t suffer if you forget something.
There should be a public toilet on the other side of the park. Let’s see whether it is usable enough. Otherwise, we could kindly ask the pizzeria if we can use theirs and leave a tip. In any case, please use the toilet before you come, so we can postpone these options for as long as possibl ; ) 
If the tables are already occupied, we will meet inside the park instead. I will post the new location here, but we should be visible somehow.
 
Happy to see you there, Patricia 
https://maps.app.goo.gl/JXgLgWTFyomgp6T58?g_st=it

German: 
Hallo ihr Lieben, 
unser nächstes Treffen findet am Donnerstag, den 11. Juni, um 19:00 Uhr vor der Zwingli-Kirche an der Ecke Danneckerstraße/Rudolfstraße (10245) statt. (Den Link zu Google Maps findet ihr unten, danke Nikki).
Wir treffen uns an den beiden Tischen, die ihr auf dem Bild seht. Auf den Bänken finden mit wenig Liebe 8 Leute, mit etwas mehr Liebe 12 Leute, und mit ganz viel Liebe sogar noch mehr Leute Platz. Ich kann 2–4 Klappstühle mitbringen, wenn mir jemand hilft, sie von der Simon-Dach-Straße hin und her zu tragen. 
Ich bringe auch Tischdecken und ein paar romantische Kleinigkeiten mit. Bringt gerne Getränke und Essen mit. Der nächste Späti ist etwa 3 Minuten zu Fuß entfernt, falls ihr etwas vergessen solltet. 
Auf der anderen Seite des Parks befindet sich eine öffentliche Toilette. Mal sehen, ob sie benutzbar genug ist. Andernfalls könnten wir in der Pizzeria nebenan höflich fragen, ob wir ihre Toilette benutzen dürfen, und dort ein Trinkgeld hinterlassen. Bitte geht auf die Toilette, bevor ihr kommt, damit wir diese Optionen so lange wie möglich hinauszögern können.
Falls die Tische bereits besetzt sind, treffen wir uns stattdessen im Park. Ich werde den neuen Treffpunkt hier posten, aber wir sollten leicht zu finden sein.
Ich freue mich schon sehr darauf, euch wiederzusehen, 
Patricia 
https://maps.app.goo.gl/JXgLgWTFyomgp6T58?g_st=it

[2026-06-03] Open Call for Bazaar Artists and Makers
Laschian Collective x Spreemarkt at Holzmarkt

Hey beautiful people,

we are happy to announce that Laschian Collective is collaborating with Spreemarkt at Holzmarkt for a special cultural market edition.

During a time when visibility, connection, and solidarity feel especially important, we want to create a space where culture can be seen, shared, and celebrated in all its diversity.

A day shaped by art, music, food, workshops, performance, and community.

For our bazaar, we are looking for artists, designers, makers, and small independent brands who would like to present and sell their work.

Date: Saturday, 13 June
Time: 12:00 to 20:00
Location: Holzmarkt, Berlin

Bazaar spaces

Table without roof protection
220 x 75 cm
30 € gross

Market stall with roof
2 metres
45 € gross

Market stall with roof
3 metres
55 € gross

For food stands, there is no fixed stall fee. Instead, Holzmarkt receives 15 percent of the sales revenue.

After your participation has been confirmed, we kindly ask you to pay a 10 € reservation fee. This amount will be deducted from the final stall fee.

In case of cancellation, the 10 € reservation fee is nonrefundable.

We are looking for around 5 to 8 artists and retailers from our community. Handmade objects, prints, jewellery, textiles, ceramics, illustrations, books, vintage pieces, small design products, and personal creations are all welcome.

There are only five uncovered tables available, so please let us know soon which option you would prefer.

To apply, send us:

• a short description of your work
• one or two photos
• your Instagram page or website, if available
• your preferred stall size

We would love to fill the market with the energy, creativity, and voices of our community.

Write us directly if you would like to join or have any questions.

Love is the answer,
Laschian Collective

[2026-06-02] Want to host an event of any kind? 
The KiezPlatz program is open! 

We provide: a speaker, some very basic cozyness, and a self-reliant space in the middle of the action sheltered from sun and rain that's open for whatever you want from 9am to 9pm.

You provide: whatever you want! There is a lot of space on top of the stage and the floor should be suitable for dancing workshops, movement things, but also talks and random shenanigans. If you need any more complex set up than a JBL Charge 6 speaker, it might need to be BYO unless we source one from the community. 

There's no application process. Just write your event on [this sheet](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1Tweb4vTxkDyoMx--VfYXBR2Rlms80FsAX1F4QKjuTcs/edit?usp=sharing) or directly on the blackboard on site and show up ❤️ if you want your event to be on the printed program, put it on the sheet by June 7th! 

⭐ I'm also still looking for helpers to source cozyness and some basic tech. If you can help or if your camp has stuff in storage they won't need this year, pm me or join this [signal chat!](https://signal.group/#CjQKIDEkFnuOUWMWUuaq7gu3jhCsj7Wclzl9JX_mwsn1U9ztEhDgJVkFSwiyoh4OyVdfa2zb)

[2026-05-29] **Help wanted to revive the big stage!**

Do you remember the big, mostly unused stage in central playa? I'd love to turn it into a collective, decentralized, BYO community space that doesn't belong to any one camp but is available for anyone to offer workshops and events before the firespace opens. It's way too big to be used as a stage, but it would be a lovely shaded/rain protected space for anything we can dream of! Loosely inspired by the Middle of Nowhere :)
My dream is to provide:

very basic infrastructure: a speaker, a mic, some carpets/pillows/soft sitting space on the stage.
a sign-up sheet (both in advance and a printed "immediacy sheet" to reserve a slot on the spot)

...and let the community make of the space what they would like.

My capacity is really limited, so I need some help!

❤️ Humans that can help one afternoon of build 
❤️ Humans that want to host events

[2026-05-27] ✨ ECSTATIC DANCE ✨
Cacao • Breath • Movement • Release

📍 Sha-La Waterfront Kreuzberg
🗓 Saturday, May 30
🕖 Doors open 19:15

An evening to land in the body, move freely, and reconnect through music, breath, cacao, and dance.

We begin softly together in a circle with cacao, a short meditation, gentle breath practices, and one or two simple songs before opening the space into a freeform ecstatic dance journey.

No choreography.
No pressure.
No “right” way to move.

Just music, presence, release, beautiful humans, and permission to dance honestly.

Some dance wildly.
Some close their eyes.
Some laugh.
Some cry.
Some remember what it feels like to feel fully alive again.

✨ First time? Many people come alone and no dance experience is needed.

[2026-05-27] Vor der HoeppnerStraße 83 ist ein Container mit einem Lattenrost und einem Holzbett in gutem Zustand.

[2026-05-27] From sharing group:

[2026-05-27] Yeah that they turn off the energy is very rare. You'd start out in the expensive base tariff but you can often also apply for your move in date in retrospect for your cheaper contract. So even if you only apply on the 5th the contract can still start on the 1st (i believe).

[2026-05-27] If the local utility company (Stadtwerke) knows that your previous tenant is moving out and that’s the only reason the contract was terminated, everything’s fine.

By default, you’ll always be supplied under the utility company’s standard tariff, no matter what else happens.
But this standard tariff is quite expensive.

If you’re looking for the absolute cheapest electricity tariff, use a price comparison site (or several)
And if green energy is important to you, I highly recommend Bürgerwerke – that’s where I’m with too.
They’re a consortium of several very small plants, such as a village’s small wind turbine. But they also include a large hydroelectric power station.

[2026-05-27] Looking for advice. Moving into a flat, and the previous tenant's electricity is due to be turned off on the 31st. (Berliner Stadtwerke). 
What's the best way to make sure that the power doesn't stop. And should I change providers? What's your experience

[2026-05-24] **34m² flat in Kreuzberg, **free from** June 1st** for 2-7 months

I'm helping a friend find a temporary subtenant, ideally from June first. Details: 

• Located in Kreuzberg, close to Kottbusser Tor
• Rent is 645€ incl everything, deposit is €1500 ideally
• One large bedroom / living room, small kitchen, bathroom with bath tub, balcony with pretty amazing views (11th floor)

Note that:
• It's above a busy street, you often hear car/truck noises (even when windows are closed), and sometimes people yelling. One of the noisier flats in Berlin, though not as bad as living opposite a Karaoke bar. 
• Kottbusser Tor is an area with many homeless people, some of which appear mentally unstable. I and all other people who lived there so far (incl. women) felt safe, it's a busy street, and no-one I know ever got attacked or anything (people would only asked me for cigarettes or money sometimes), but if you're the type of person who feels stressed at Kottbusser Tor at night, or does not like "Kotti aesthetics", this might not be the place for you. On the upside: Very central, well-connected with U1, U3, U8, lots of amazing food and some nice bars etc within just 50m from your door 🙂

**Interested? **Message me and please include: 

1) start your message with "Burner Kottiflat [move in date]"
2) Can you pay rent from June 1st onwards? If not, when is the earliest you could pay rent from? How long do you want to stay? (min/max)
3) Can you pay €1500 deposit? If not, how much can you pay?
4) Would you move in alone, with a friend/partner (that's fine), or with a pet (depends)
5) Do you need Anmeldung? (probably hard to get, I can check)
6) if we don't already know each other, what's your full name, do we have any mutuals? (You can check my [Linkedin](https://www.linkedin.com/in/manuelallgaier), [Facebook](https://www.facebook.com/manuel2103), shared Telegram groups). Copy/paste messages fine too, I know flat-hunting sucks and want to make this as easy as possible.
7) Your phone number and best way to reach you (Whatsapp/SMS/calls preferred)
😍 Any questions you might have 

FAQ: Yes, it's still available, I'll remove this post when it's taken 🙂 

Hope this helps out someone!

A conscious evening of movement, music, presence, and connection.

**
We are currently living as a small, committed community in a house in Berlin that is likely to be sold – and we are actively looking for a buyer who resonates with our vision.

What we’re looking for:
A buyer / investor who sees this as a solid capital investment and at the same time is open to supporting a long-term, community-based living project.

Who we are:
– A reliable group of tenants who want to stay long-term
– We have independently renovated and maintained the house over the past years
– We genuinely enjoy taking care of the space and are motivated to continue improving and increasing its value in cooperation
– We value responsible, respectful and community-oriented living

What this offers you:
– A stable capital investment with committed, long-term tenants
– People who actively care for, develop and upgrade the property
– A collaborative setup based on trust, communication and shared interest in maintaining value

What we’re looking to build:
A relationship that is
– fair and cooperative
– long-term oriented
– and aligned with both economic sustainability and social value

If this speaks to you – or if you know someone who might be interested – we’d love to hear from you.

Happy to share more details about the house and us in a personal conversation.

[2026-05-06] Might be relevant for some of you:
**🇪🇺 European Citizens' Initiative: Suspend the EU-Israel Agreement**

The European Commission itself has held Israel responsible for the mass killing of civilians, the destruction of hospitals, and the blockade of humanitarian aid in Gaza — which may constitute the use of starvation as a method of war. The International Court of Justice has also ordered Israel to prevent genocide.

Despite this, the EU has not yet suspended its association agreement with Israel — the cornerstone of trade and political cooperation between the two parties.

A European Citizens' Initiative is calling for exactly that: the full suspension of this agreement. Already **over 1.17 million people** have signed. The target is 1.5 million signatures (a minimum of 1 million valid signatures across at least 7 EU countries is required for official validity).

✍️ Sign here:
https://citizens-initiative.europa.eu/initiatives/details/2025/000005_en

[2026-05-04] Hello dears,

I’m offering an electronic live music masterclass on May 19 at Ableton HQ in Berlin. It is an in-depth look at my live looped vocal downtempo set, Particle Twirl.
I’ll demonstrate the set-up in Ableton Live, my effects and mixing chain, my signal routing, and the individual vocal effects I use to manipulate my voice live. I’ll also introduce my MIDI controllers and their mappings, which allows my setup to fit into a backpack despite its complexity. Depending on the participants, this masterclass will be held in English or German.

Tickets are only 22 Euros - I’d love to see some of you there! https://www.eventbrite.de/e/electronic-live-music-with-ableton-live-a-masterclass-with-juc-tickets-1986897114756

[2026-05-04] Divine Pleasure Journey🌈 Beginner Friendly

📅 Sa, 16.05. 
📍 Leipzig, Schleußig 
🕓 18:00–23:30 Uhr (Ankommen ab 17:45 Uhr)

Die Divine Pleasure Journey ist ein bewusst gehaltener Raum für queere, offene und neugierige Menschen, die Berührung, Nähe und klare Kommunikation erforschen wollen. 

Ich halte seit vielen Jahren Räume zu Embodiment, Grenzen, Kommunikation und Gruppenprozessen. Gemeinsam mit meinem Angel-Team sorge ich für einen sicheren, zugänglichen Rahmen, in dem du dich frei bewegen kannst. 

Ich möchte dich mit meinen Räumen ermutigen, klarer zu deinem Nein stehen zu können, dein Herz berühren, dass Sexualität nicht Scham behaftet sein sollte und du dich frei entfalten darfst! Wie wäre ein Space, in dem du durch den Raum gleiten kannst, in deinem Tempo, dich inspirieren lassen darfst und das Wort MÜSSEN UND SCHNELL zu Hause bleibt. Ich möchte den Alltag entschleunigen und dir helfen, wieder in dein Inneres zu finden. 

Es ist diesmal ein nicht penetrativer Raum.

🌀 Ablauf

🕟 17:45–18:00 – Ankommen
🔻 18:00–18:30 – Meditation& KAKAO ZEREMONIE MIT ROH KAKAO 

🛡 18:30-19:00 – Consent, Hygiene, Agreements
Klare Regeln, gemeinsame Sprache, sichere Kommunikationsformen.

🎲 19:00-22:00– Verspielte Körperübungen & Connection Games
Berührung, Nähe, Slow Play, Präsenz.
Mit ca. 30 Minuten Essens- und Trinkpause.

🌌 22:00- 23:30 – Open Space
Freie Exploration: Touch, Gespräche, Experimentieren, Rückzugsmöglichkeiten – alles auf Basis von klaren Ja/Nein-Kommunikationen.

✨ ca. 23:30 – Closing

👗 Dresscode

Komme so, wie du dich frei, mutig, expressiv oder einfach wohlfühlst:
Mesh, Samt, Harness, Glitzer, Satin, weiche Stoffe, Playwear, Kimono, Leinenhose 
Keine Streetwear.
Umkleideraum vorhanden.

🎒 Was du mitbringen kannst

• Handtuch oder Sarong
• Augenmaske
• Trinkflasche
• vegetarisches Buffetbeitrag (bitte kein Knoblauch)

Früchte, Tee und Wasser gibt’s vor Ort.

Hinweis

Bitte teste dich regelmäßig auf STIs.
Es schafft Sicherheit für dich und alle Menschen im Raum und ist ein zentraler Teil von verantwortungsvollem Consent.


💸 Beitrag: 60€ pro Person


📩 Anmeldung

Schreib mir eine Nachricht mit ein paar Worten zu dir und was Konsens für dich bedeutet (mind. 200 Zeichen).
Wenn du schon einmal dabei warst, reicht eine kurze Nachricht. Bitte beachte, dass ich auf eine gute Balance im Raum achte und dadurch nicht alle Menschis angenommen werden können 🫶🏽

🎟 Keine Rückgabe oder Weitergabe der Tickets möglich.

Ich freue mich sehr auf diesen Abend mit euch! 

Eure Jules 💋

[2026-04-30] Thats horrible and terrifying. What is wrong with people?? Glad you were okay.

[2026-04-30] Finally somebody took "Safety Third" seriously!!

[2026-04-30] especially after that massive fire in switzerland that you mentioned and considering that (if i'm not misremembering, lmk if this isn't a fact) there was a fire at JK a few years ago already i find that reaction from staff surprising. very safety fifth.

[2026-04-30] Hey everyone, I just want to let you know about something seriously dangerous that happened at Jonny Knüppel last weekend - especially if you are planning to go there tomorrow for May 1st. 

At about 5:00AM on Sunday morning, a woman set off a fountain firework in the middle of an indoor dancefloor. I’m talking a steady stream of flame, fire and sparks for 1 whole minute - with sparks so high they were hitting and bouncing off the ceiling. The room was totally crowded and foggy, and the exits were not visible from where I was standing. The woman was clearly high on k and unresponsive; her friends were equally nonchalant.

Someone set off an identical firework inside a bar in Switzerland just 4 months ago, resulting in a fire that killed 41 people and caused over 115 burns and injuries. 

Needless to say I was absolutely terrified. I went to tell a security guard what happened, and to ask for the woman to be removed from the club. The security guard went to go talk to the woman. As this was happening, I was feeling so shaken that I decided to leave. On my way out, I saw the security guard again at the entrance who said, "I have spoken to the woman and she will not do it again." I said "OK, thank you" and walked out. However, this was a completely unacceptable response from the security at Jonny Knüppel. They did not react with the seriousness the situation required.

I warn people to really be careful there. Always have access to an exit. They do not care nearly enough for people’s safety and they don’t take violations seriously!

[2026-04-29] The recent decision by the Bundesgerichtshof expands the scope for “Eigenbedarfskündigung” — evictions based on personal use — and shifts the balance further toward property owners.

We keep hearing the same refrain: let prices rise, and the market will respond by building more housing. But that theory collapses in reality. What we are seeing instead is not a surge of affordable construction, but a system where thousands of individual landlords act in parallel, pushing rents ever higher.

This is not a healthy market. It behaves like a cartel — fragmented on paper, unified in effect — where rising prices are not corrected by competition, but reinforced by it.

The result is a city where housing is treated less as a basic need and more as a speculative asset. And the people who live here are left competing not just for homes, but against a system designed to extract as much as possible from them.

Ho’oponopono is an ancient Hawaiian practice of forgiveness and reconciliation. Traditionally, it means “to make right” with oneself and with others. It is understood as a way of bringing healing not only to present relationships, but also to ancestral and family lines, clearing what is incomplete so greater peace, freedom, and alignment can emerge

📅 June 1st – mid-August (flexible)

[2026-04-27] Dear friends, 

After some internal discussions, Musotopia has decided to take a little pause from Kiez Burn this year. 


We have joined every edition of Kiez Burn since 2019, with the dream of having more live music in a burn and creating a space where the community could express themselves through rhythm, melodies, questionable dance moves, and magic shared moments.  
We really loved every minute of it and we will sincerely miss being there with all of you this year.


Over time, a few things have changed: the move to a new location, the increasingly strict sound regulations, and the gentle migration of sound camps further and further into the land of whispers. Bringing up to last year having our camp situated in a quiet zone. We fully understand the need for balance, but we would be lying if we said we don’t miss the more expressive, free and spontaneous magic of earlier years.

So we felt this was the right moment to pause, recalibrate, and gather some fresh energy, so we can return in future years stronger, brighter (and with more bass!)


Our wish remains the same: to create a beautiful space for music, dancing, connection, spontaneous joy, and self-expression.  While still keeping our cozy tent alive for chill sounds, jam sessions, and late-night conversations, we will come back in 2027 with a more dancefloor oriented concept.

Sending you lot of love ! 
Your dear Schmusos 🌹

[2026-04-26] 30.04. 19:00 Lecture “How to Stay Grounded in Uncertain Times”
Life can feel overwhelming when everything around is unstable. In this session, as a rehabilitational psychologist (Ms) I will share practical tools from psychology to help you stay grounded, regulate anxiety, and regain a sense of control.
We’ll explore:
- How the brain reacts to uncertainty and stress
- Why we get stuck in panic and overthinking cycles
- Wide range of techniques to calm and regulate your nervous system
- How to support yourself and people close to you
The session combines insights from rehabilitation psychology with practical, easy-to-use methods you can apply immediately.
PAKD Gallery (An d Mole 9, Ostkreutz, Berlin)
7€ (pre-registration) / 10€ at the door

[2026-04-25] Potential allergy information from ingredients would be rather important to share with your participants, mind you.

Also. There is no such thing as a product with no downsides. Generally safe in most situations, at certain amounts, sure, but there will always be people who react badly to certain things at certain quantities. I'm sure you're aware, but it doesn't sit right to claim something (especially something with limited exposure to the larger population so far) is completely safe. Does not give a lot of confidence in participant safety.

[2026-04-24] Prrrr hi hi magical souls 💛 wish you feel the magic inside of you for today annnnd a little invite ✨✨✨Ecstatic Dance • Breath • Cacao • Movement  
@ Sha-La Waterfront, Kreuzberg

Hey you ✨

On April 25th, we gather for an Ecstatic Dance at Sha-La Waterfront — a 3-hour journey into movement, presence, and connection.

This evening is an invitation to step out of the everyday and into your body.  
To slow down, to listen, and to meet yourself — just as you are, in this moment.

We begin gently with cacao and a guided breath practice, allowing the body to soften and the mind to settle. From there, the space opens into a dance journey shaped by music, rhythm, and presence.

There is no choreography.  
No performance.  
Nothing to prove.

Instead, you’re invited to move in a way that feels natural to you — whether that’s dancing, exploring, resting, or simply being. You can stay in your own world or connect with others, always within a space that is held with awareness and respect.

The music will guide us through different layers — from subtle and spacious, into playful and expressive, into deeper intensity, and back into stillness. Each phase offers a different doorway into your own experience.

We close the evening with a short integration, creating space to land, receive, and let the experience settle in the body.

✨ What to expect:
• Ceremonial cacao  
• Breath & energy attunement  
• Ecstatic Dance journey (DJ set by Sebastiaan Lefuce)  
• Integration & rest  

No previous dance experience is needed.  
Come as you are and move in your own rhythm.

[2026-04-22] Hi friends, I am drowning and reaching out for support

Some of you may know me through Kiez Burn, some of you might not. It's been an absolute joy being a part of the e.V. board these past few months, and I am constantly amazed by the power of our community. Honestly, I'm embarrassed to post this, but it's one of the few extra things I can do right now.

My father, Donald Romanello, passed away unexpectedly last week in the US. I'm back in Boston now, and with each day, I am realizing the insane financial burden of even a basic funeral and fees to get his life in order. As an only child to a divorced parent, this is all on me.

My dad was an amazing human. A gender-nonconforming, queer soul who only felt comfortable coming out to me in the last 10 years of his life. A disabled person struggling with his own financial hardship, yet always had an open heart and felt things intensely - just like me. 

But mostly, he was a hippie who loved music, art, and traveling. Maybe you caught me wheeling him around Neukölln last year ❤️ He is the reason I am a part of the burner community, and he loved hearing my tales of Kiez Burns past. He even donated his old Postal Service uniforms to us at the Prost Office kiez in 2023.

I can't sum up his life here - I've written more about him and the situation on this [memorial page](https://everloved.com/life-of/donald-romanello/?flow=201). 

I know everyone is struggling right now. If you've read this far, thank you. If you have something extra to spare, thank you. If you don't, please don't worry - just knowing my dad's story is heard is already a huge support. 

I love you, thank you ❤️ -Amy

[2026-04-15] Starseeders & Institute Casa de Cura invite you to

Flowing: A Planet Water Evening
📆 May 4 · 18:00–00:00
UHU Salon, Berlin

In a world that has forgotten its essence, join us for an enchanting evening honoring the sacred element that sustains us—WATER. Step into an oasis of connection where dialogue, presence and art converge to rekindle our relationship with the water that gives life.

Featuring:
- Laitti (Bia Paiva) — Water meditations, infusions & guided activations. A visionary catalyst for transformation and community healing, bringing 20+ years of practice bridging humanity and nature through art, philosophy and ancestral wisdom.
- Tchowa — Medicine man rooted in Lakota traditions, offering drums and sacred songs dedicated to water.
- Derya Celikkol — Immersive theatrical performance “A Love Letter to Water.”
- Nicola Bisset & Sweet Potato Gentleman — “Fluid Tension”: live AV performance exploring the life and confining journeys of water.
- Saraa Alena — Somatic movement & sound: “Connecting to Inner Waters.”
- Luca — Lomi‑Lomi & conscious touch sessions (in training).
+ Our dedicated team hosting the night.

Program
18:00 Doors open
18:30 Blue Lotus Infusion w/ Laitti
19:30 Water Activation w/ Laitti + Drumming & Singing w/ Tchowa
20:30 Papyrus Infusion w/ Laitti
21:00 A Love Letter to Water — Derya Celikkol
21:15 Fluid Tension — Nicola Bisset & Sweet Potato Gentleman (AV)
21:30 Connecting to Inner Waters — Saraa Alena (somatic movement & sound)
22:30 Last Infusion + Sharing Circle
Throughout the evening: Lomi‑Lomi massage with Luca

About the performances: experience ritual, sound, movement and audiovisual work that trace water’s journeys — from ancient seas to present streams, from inner emotion to collective healing.

A soli party for Planet Water
This evening is a gathering where love meets purpose. All profits support the Planet Water project.

Suggested donation: €30–€50
Please register with Laitti via Telegram @[user].xyz or WhatsApp +55 11 99889‑6094.
Learn more: www.casadecura.ong.br/planet-water

Bring an open heart. Together we’ll remember that we are, indeed, made of water.

(Practicals: bring your bathrobe, towel & cash)

With love,
Laitti, Tchowa, Derya, Nicola, Sweet Potato Gentleman, Saraa, Luca, Alisa & Linh

(Questions or accessibility needs? Reply here and we’ll assist.)

[2026-04-14] Sanftmut Deluxe 2.0 - Leipzig 

Die letzten zehn Tinder Matches waren mal wieder ein Reinfall?
Das neue Jahr ist schon da und irgendwo zwischen Hoffnung und Augenrollen taucht diese Frage auf:
Wo bleiben eigentlich meine Frühlingsgefühle?

Sanftmut Deluxe

Ein Raum, der dir praktische Impulse und Erfahrungen mitgibt, um Dating spielerischer, entspannter und gleichzeitig tiefer zu gestalten.
Ohne endlosen Smalltalk über Jobs, Sternzeichen oder Lieblingsmusik.

Du bestimmst selbst, wie viel du von dir zeigen möchtest.
Du darfst neugierig sein, weich werden, authentisch bleiben.
Und vielleicht begegnest du hier jemandem, der nach derselben Art von Kontakt offen ist, wie du.

Wichtig dabei:
Es geht nicht darum, jemanden finden zu müssen.
Sondern darum, dir selbst und anderen ehrlich zu begegnen.

Das Format ist queerfreundlich und bewusst nicht heteronormativ gestaltet.
Ich verbinde Elemente aus Authentic Relating, Deep Dating und Embodiment zu einem Erfahrungsraum, in dem Nähe entstehen darf, ohne Druck, ohne Rollen, ohne Ziel. Es wird keine intensive Berührung oder Sexualität geben. 


Wann? 30.04. Start 18 Uhr
Dauer ca 2 bis 2,5 Stunden
Leipzig, Ort nach Anmeldung

Beitrag

30 € pro Person

Bei Anmeldung bis 16.04.  
25 € pro Person

[2026-04-12] Hello Lovelies,

Join us for an evening of intuitive movement and surrender into expression this Sunday May 3rd, 7pm at IKSK.

Tandava is a tantric movement meditation that embodies Shiva's Cosmic Dance of the eternal rythm of creation and destruction.

This practice guides you out of your mind and into your body, inviting you to follow it's natural impulses.
Throught breath, sound, movement and touch, you enter a state of effortless flow, where the body moves you.
As you surrender to the body's innate wisdom, it naturally goes into expression, releasing stress and tention while opening up for self-healing, peace, joy and the pleasure of being in your body.

[2026-04-11] Are you a traveling artist or human coming to Berlin? 

Qaali Studio offers a private bedroom and 90 sqm of shared creative space in the heart of Berlin — open to artists and travellers who want somewhere more alive than a hotel.

The studio is dense with carpets, warmth, and tools. There's a kitchen, a sauna, a DJ setup, room to move and make things, rehearse and dance. Whether you're deep in a project or just passing through the city, you're welcome to work, rest, and be inspired here.

Affordable short stays and longer residencies available. Get in touch to book.

Tell your friends. Tell your lovers. 🤍

[2026-04-11] I think that's certainly one way a person could choose to interact with a burn. 

If someone would rather consume a "canned" experience prepared by other people, rather than creating something themselves, that's often possible. Meaningful engagement is voluntary, and especially at larger burns, there's really not a gate-keeping mechanism to try to prevent people from being passive consumers. 

The term "sparkle pony" might often be applied to people having a canned summer of love experience.

[2026-04-11] was just thinking.. A burn is like a canned version of the summer of love for the masses

[2026-04-10] ✨ Call for Performers – House of Umbra ✨

House of Umbra is an immersive installation built as a triangular prism where light, shadows, and movement merge into a living projection. Performers will dance inside the structure and their shadows will be visible to the audience.

We are currently looking for:
•⁠  ⁠Dancers
•⁠  ⁠Flow artists

When ? Saturday morning (during the « friday night ») for one of these slots : 
•⁠  ⁠Midnight-02 am : focus on flow art , gogo dance 
•⁠  ⁠⁠4-6am : dancers will dance on a set overlaid with a spoken word / poetry journey finishing with the sunrise  (all styles welcome, but also open to classical / contemporary / partner dance here )

If you’d like to perform and be part of this collaborative experience, please fill out the form:

[2026-04-08] 🌟Einladung Offline-Wandertag am Sonntag, den 12.04.🌟

Wir alle merken, wie sehr Social Media uns die Aufmerksamkeit raubt und uns nach stundenlangen doomscrollen leerer zurück lässt, als ein Tag voller Überstunden in der Bib oder am Schreibtisch. Trotzdem greifen wir wieder zum Handy. Vielleicht weil uns die Alternative fehlt?🤔

Da kommt unser Wandertag ins Spiel. Gemeinsam wollen wir den Frühling und die frische Luft genießen und den Kopf freikriegen. Und: Wir wollen zusammen überlegen, wie es besser gehen kann. Warum nimmt Social Media so viel Raum ein und was macht das mit uns? Was muss sich ändern und wie kommen wir da hin?

Dein Handy kannst du für den Zeitraum gerne bei uns abgeben oder es gleich Zuhause lassen.📵

📍Treffpunkt: Sonntag, 12. April um 12 Uhr S Grünau - Bistro Palme (Ausgang: Adlergestell) 
🗺️ Route: Wir sind ungefähr 3 Stunden zu Fuß im Naturschutzgebiet Krumme Lake unterwegs.

Denkt an wettergerechte Kleidung und bringt euch Wasser und Verpflegung für einen Mittagssnack mit.

📣 Leite diese Nachricht an deine Freunde weiter und sei dabei – aber es gilt natürlich die Regel: Bitte nichts auf Social Media über unser Event posten!📣
Wir freuen uns auf euch.🫰

__~ It’s like ecstatic dance, but with house music ~__

Do you find the concept of ecstatic dance fun, but the music is not your thing? You’re not alone. Let’s try something different together 🙌

Waves of Pleasure builds a house of sound and takes you on a journey through different expressions of house music. Together we will get high on sound (and cacao) and shake off all the worries and stress of everyday life. 

Embodied House with Sophie Spiral aka Rhythm Witxch: This guided ecstatic house warm-up will introduce you to a variety of movement qualities that honor the Black legacies of House Music and help you learn more ways to flow with, move with, and become the rhythm.

[2026-04-02] Hello dears! I’m excited to share my new project for sex-positive humans 🤗

**“HOW TO USE ME”**

It is a pocket-size playbook with personal questions that center pleasure and joy. You can write your answers and transform this book into a manual about yourself ☀️

“How to use me” invites to reflect on and explore topics like consent, desires, boundaries, relationship agreements, safer sex, aftercare, and the unique sensitivity of your body.

**What can you do with it?**

🌸Fill it out for yourself as a tool for self-reflection and self-discovery
🌸Prepare it as a gift for your partner(s)
🌸Use it as a way introduce yourself at sex-positive events

I’d love to see it spread everywhere! (and yes, also receive some money for my work 💸). 

You can contact me and get a zine for a donation between €1–€10 (recommended donation is €5).

If you want 20+ copies for your event, we can do €3 per zine, OR you cover the materials and create a cute little “How to Use Me” station with a donation box

Please write to me if you have any feedback, questions, or suggestions! @[user]
It’s very fresh, so I appreciate any thoughts 🙏🏻 thank youuu

Hugs 🤗

[2026-04-02] Hey and thank you again for sharing this with us ❤️

We took your feedback to heart and made a few quick changes. We increased the font size on the website and also tried to make the visuals a bit clearer and easier to read where possible.

We really hope this already makes things more accessible for you and others. We know it is still quite simple and a bit improvised overall but for now we hope it is a more workable version.

We are definitely keeping this in mind for the future and will pay much more attention to accessibility as we continue building this.

Thanks again for pointing it out and for the way you shared it with us it really helped.
If you ever feel like continuing the exchange we would be very happy about that.

[2026-04-01] Well, __Comic Sans__ is a meme font for a reason: it's terrible 😅

[2026-04-01] No shade. I didn't think it was intentional. I've spent most of my life pretending I don't have a disability and would never have said anything before - but because I know it's not intentional I thought it was important to share my immediate response rather than quietly disengaging. Especially in case there are others with difficulties but not (yet) ready to say something.

Also, German itself isn't the main barrier for me personally if I'm expecting it. It's a combination of it with the difficult font.

I'm happy to engage further if you want ❤️

[2026-04-01] Thank you so much for your honest and thoughtful feedback we truly appreciate it 🙏

Our website is currently quite improvised and still very much a work in progress. At the moment it is mainly meant to give a first impression of what is emerging around the Æther Express and the kind of atmosphere we are hoping to create.

Thank you as well for helping to deepen our awareness around this. It really helps us understand more clearly how playful fonts and certain design choices can quickly become a barrier especially for people with visual impairments or when the content is not in one’s native language. We are definitely taking this to heart.

The website itself is currently in German but on our devices it can be automatically translated into other languages depending on system settings. That said we understand this is not a perfect solution and may not work equally well for everyone.

The text within the images cannot be translated directly. At the moment those are mostly in English as we are trying to speak to an international audience. We do recognize that this can also create additional barriers and we will reflect on how to improve this going forward.

We are all working on this voluntarily and none of us are professionals so many things are still evolving quite organically. This makes your feedback all the more valuable as it helps us think more inclusively and take concrete steps to improve.

If you feel open to it we would very much appreciate being in personal exchange with you. We would be happy to provide any information in your preferred language and also explore together what format would make things most accessible for you.

For the event itself we can already share that there will be little to no written content on site and that most program elements will be held in both German and English.

Thank you again for sharing your perspective it truly helps us make the Æther Express more accessible for more people 💛

[2026-04-01] Hey there. Short feedback to the website (and a general comment for all creative types):

Whimsical fonts are great as logos and in other limited places, but for those of us with bad vision, it's a real barrier to engaging with actual content. Especially when it's not in our native language. 

When I open the site, I literally can't read a word on it without zooming in and putting a lot of extra energy in. 

The result (which I know you don't intend) is that I feel this event is explicitly not for me or others with disabilities, and it makes it a lot less likely that I'll engage further, with what I assume is otherwise an objectively awesome new burn!

[2026-04-01] **Dancing in the Dark — Movement Experience with Eyes Closed**

April 26, 2026
13:00 – 15:00

Close your eyes and let the world of images fade away. With sight turned off, your other senses awaken — space feels different, people are sensed in new ways, and every movement becomes truly free. This is all about moving without judgment, self-censorship, or the need to perform, where perception sharpens and subtle sensations come to life.

We’ll begin with a gentle introduction and a short exploration of back sensitivity — awakening the skin, muscles, and deeper layers of the back through simple sensory exercises. By tuning attention to this often unseen part of the body, we open new pathways for awareness, support, and movement.

Then the playlist will guide you into your own free movement — every sigh, sway, or spin is already a dance. There are no right or wrong steps, only the chance to release what’s inside and experience the pure joy of moving unseen.

No previous experience required.
Recommended donation: €20
**Registration & details**: https://forms.gle/P7c1hm4xzcj2w3ZR9

[2026-03-29] Thanks, will try thinner thread and paper - unfortunately l tried literally all different tensions so unfortunately that's not the (solemn) solution here.

[2026-03-29] Looks like upper thread tension being too tight. Using paper/ interfacing might also help. Also special needles for thin fabric or starching the fabric to stiffen it. Or even (gasp) paper glue that comes in sticks - the goal is to make the fabric less slippery. And I would check the thread, it's hard to tell from the picture, but you might need thinner thread

[2026-03-29] Thanks l will get one and try that!

[2026-03-29] Have you considered a stepper/walking foot? This helps with stretchy and slippery fabric. 
Then slowly and small stitches

[2026-03-29] I have a Singer Tradition machine if that helps...

[2026-03-27] Hey everybody,

anybody having a **conflict** at the moment? With your partner or your team?

If so, have you ever heard about **mediation**?

A mediation is a structured process where a neutral third person supports people in conflict to communicate more clearly and understand each other’s perspectives. Instead of deciding who is right, the mediator helps them find their own workable solution.

I am about to end my mediation training  and I am offering some mediation session for expense allowance.

Please write me a DM if you are interested.

Best Basta

**
Dancing Water | Fusion of Persian & Mallorca rhythms, poetry, & dances

We invite you to a unique experience of mystical music, narrative dances, and shared stories, inspired by Persia, the Mediterranean, & Southern Spain. 

The night begins with atmospheric dj sets of ethnic Mediterranean & Persian sounds, with a small bar serving you drinks & a taste of Iran traditional food. [2026-03-22] Hi! I'm Tsubasa, Burning Japan organizer joining KiezBurn 2026 as Effigy Lead 🤠
This year we are building an octopus in a truly collaborative, decentralized fashion — 8 arms, each one representing, owned and shaped by a different community that is a part of KB. 

To this group, I have a request/invitation: I am looking for someone to lead the **Ecology arm** —I think this one's yours😁💚 I think this topic is particularly important, and we don't it give nearly enough attention at burns.

I want this effigy to be a *representation of the diversity, power, resilience, and possibilities in this community of communities.*
Therefore, each arm  has its own aesthetic, its own lead, its own story. The body's metachrosis - enabled by live projection/VJ - allows the octopus to camouflage, melding deeper into the microcosm of Deutsch Gegenkultur.

As a Tentacle Lead, the work would be to birth one arm — its aesthetic, its story, its experience. The structural skeleton and core materials are provided; everything else is yours to imagine and execute. You'll develop your concept at your own pace, optionally prototype at a makerspace/workshop in early June, then build it out during build week. Occasional check-ins (~monthly) keep you in the loop without eating your life. Otherwise: your arm, your call.

Build week is **June 18–22**. Burn is **June 23–29**.

We have a strong "don't burn yourself out" policy; do what you want and can - everything else is a conversation, including the scope of these roles.

Please DM me if **any** of this sparks interest, and share with anyone that you think would resonate.

**Thank you for time, and power to you!**

[2026-03-21] Also, there is no right and wrong. You will forget things at home, you will misunderstand cultural stuff specific to Borderland culture. It's okay ❤️ Sometimes there are virgin onboardings or something like that. Going to local meet ups can also be a very good place to meet people who are going to the event or have been before. 
In terms of getting there finding a rideshare is your best option to bring a comfortable amount of camping gear. It's possible to do it with just what you can carry, but you might struggle with lack of comfort at some point. Soft mattress are heavy, so is a good sleeping bag. In terms of camps, make sure you stay tuned on Discord to see if there is camp matchmaking somewhere. Otherwise again go to local meetings and ask around. The last question was how you can contribute. No matter where and how you end up camping, doing shifts is always great to feel you're a part of the event and to get to know people. I would recommend clown police or gate as most virgin friendly, unless you have special medical/psychological welfare knowledge. The day shifts in the early week always go fill up quickly, so make sure to sign up fast. 
Otherwise have fun finding your way, which will be completely different to other people's way. Listen to yourself and have lots of fun!
